x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x41\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x4D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x54\x65\x78\x74\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x5F\x54\x65\x78\x74\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x6E\x65\x72\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x6C\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x6C\x69\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x62\x61\x63\x6B\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x6E\x64\x2D\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x28\x32\x35\x35\x2C\x32\x35\x35\x2C\x32\x35\x35\x29\x22\x5D\x20\x2E\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x2C\x2E\x64\x68\x5F\x6E\x65\x77\x5F\x6D\x65\x64\x69\x61\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x61\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x2A\x2C\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x62\x75\x64\x64\x79\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x2A\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x68\x61\x6E\x64\x6C\x65\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x6E\x61\x6D\x65\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x61\x73\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x22\x5D\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x65\x65\x64\x62\x61\x63\x6B\x5F\x73\x68\x6F\x77\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x67\x65\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x2E\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x2E\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x63\x61\x6C\x6C\x74\x6F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x2E\x73\x65\x65\x4D\x6F\x72\x65\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x6C\x69\x6B\x65\x74\x65\x78\x74\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x74\x69\x63\x6B\x65\x72\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x42\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x74\x72\x65\x61\x6D\x4D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x20\ x61\x79\x44\x61\x72\x6B\x54\x6F\x70\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x20\x3E\x20\x2E\x55\x49\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x20\x2E\x64\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x2D\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x6C\x79\x6F\x75\x74\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x46\x61\x63\x65\x70\x69\x6C\x65\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x20\x2E\x75\x69\x54\x6F\x6F\x6C\x74\x69\x70\x57\x72\x61\x70\x20\x7B\x62\x6F\x78\x2D\x73\x68\x61\x64\x6F\x77\x3A\x20\x30\x20\x30\x20\x31\x65\x6D\x20\x31\x70\x78\x20\x23\x30\x30\x30\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x2E\x65\x78\x74\x72\x61\x5F\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x73\x20\x75\x6C\x20\x6C\x69\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x52\x6F\x75\x6E\x64\x65\x64\x42\x6F\x78\x5F\x42\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x5F\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x5F\x6C\x6F\x67\x6F\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x65\x64\x2C\x23\x70\x72\x65\x73\x65\x6E\x63\x65\x5F\x6E\x6F\x74\x69\x66\x69\x63\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x2C\x23\x63\x68\x61\x74\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x62\x61\x72\x78\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x5F\x64\x69\x76\x2C\x2E\x70\x6C\x61\x79\x73\x5F\x76\x61\x6C\x2C\x20\x23\x6D\x61\x69\x6C\x42\x6F\x78\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x73\x20\x6C\x69\x20\x61\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x62\x75\x64\x64\x79\x5F\x72\x6F\x77\x20\x61\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x62\x75\x64\x64\x79\x52\x6F\x77\x20\x61\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x6E\x61\x76\x69\x67\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x20\x61\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x70\x72\x65\x73\x65\x6E\x63\x65\x5F\x61\x70\x70\x6C\x69\x63\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x2C\x23\x62\x75\x64\x64\x79\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x2C\x23\x70\x72\x65\x73\x65\x6E\x63\x65\x5F\x65\x72\x72\x6F\x72\x5F\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x74\x65\x70\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x20\x2E\x6D\x69\x64\x64\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x6A\x65\x77\x65\x6C\ x69\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x29\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x50\x72\x69\x76\x61\x63\x79\x57\x69\x64\x67\x65\x74\x20\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x29\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x53\x75\x70\x70\x72\x65\x73\x73\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x41\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x4D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x53\x75\x70\x70\x72\x65\x73\x73\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6E\x6E\x65\x63\x74\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x72\x6F\x6C\x73\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x20\x2E\x75\x69\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x66\x62\x44\x6F\x63\x6B\x43\x68\x61\x74\x44\x72\x6F\x70\x64\x6F\x77\x6E\x29\x20\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x75\x69\x43\x6C\x6F\x73\x65\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x29\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x52\x69\x62\x62\x6F\x6E\x2C\x23\x66\x62\x44\x6F\x63\x6B\x43\x68\x61\x74\x42\x75\x64\x64\x79\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x4E\x75\x62\x20\x2E\x66\x62\x4E\x75\x62\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x70\x6C\x75\x67\x69\x6E\x52\x65\x63\x6F\x6D\x6D\x65\x6E\x64\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x42\x61\x72\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x4C\x69\x6B\x65\x20\x7B\x62\x6F\x78\x2D\x73\x68\x61\x64\x6F\x77\x3A\x20\x30\x20\x30\x20\x2E\x35\x65\x6D\x20\x72\x67\x62\x61\x28\x30\x2C\x30\x2C\x30\x2C\x30\x2E\x39\x29\x2C\x69\x6E\x73\x65\x74\x20\x30\x20\x30\x20\x2E\x37\x35\x65\x6D\x20\x23\x39\x63\x66\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x62\x6F\x72\x64\x65\x72\x2D\x77\x69\x64\x74\x68\x3A\x20\x30\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x20\x7D\x0A\x0A\x2E\x66\x62\x43\x68\x61\x74\x42\x75\x64\x64\x79\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x44\x72\x6F\x70\x64\x6F\x77\x6E\x20\x2E\x75\x69\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x65\ x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x73\x75\x62\x6D\x69\x74\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x6F\x6D\x6F\x74\x65\x5F\x70\x61\x67\x65\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x63\x72\x65\x61\x74\x65\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x73\x68\x61\x72\x65\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x5F\x62\x72\x6F\x77\x73\x65\x72\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x73\x69\x6C\x76\x65\x72\x5F\x63\x72\x65\x61\x74\x65\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x5F\x73\x68\x65\x6C\x6C\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x69\x6E\x74\x65\x64\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x6C\x79\x65\x72\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x63\x6C\x6F\x73\x65\x29\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x29\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x76\x69\x64\x65\x6F\x69\x63\x6F\x6E\x29\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x61\x73\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x29\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x47\x42\x53\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x42\x6F\x78\x5F\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x67\x73\x57\x72\x61\x70\x70\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6E\x6E\x65\x63\x74\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x72\x6F\x6C\x73\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x20\x2E\x75\x69\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x66\x62\x44\x6F\x63\x6B\x43\x68\x61\x74\x44\x72\x6F\x70\x64\x6F\x77\x6E\x29\x20\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x75\x69\x43\x6C\x6F\x73\x65\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x29\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x4D\x6F\x72\x65\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x66\x62\x44\x6F\x63\x6B\x43\x68\x61\x74\x42\x75\x64\x64\x79\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x4E\x75\x62\x20\x2E\x66\x62\x4E\x75\x62\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\ x34\x70\x78\x20\x38\x70\x78\x20\x23\x39\x63\x66\x3B\x70\x61\x64\x64\x69\x6E\x67\x3A\x20\x30\x20\x34\x70\x78\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x23\x66\x62\x5F\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x62\x61\x72\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x6F\x67\x72\x65\x73\x73\x5F\x62\x61\x72\x5F\x6F\x75\x74\x65\x72\x20\x7B\x62\x6F\x78\x2D\x73\x68\x61\x64\x6F\x77\x3A\x20\x69\x6E\x73\x65\x74\x20\x30\x20\x30\x20\x33\x70\x78\x20\x23\x30\x30\x30\x2C\x30\x20\x30\x20\x33\x65\x6D\x20\x33\x70\x78\x20\x23\x30\x30\x30\x3B\x7D\x0A\x23\x70\x72\x65\x73\x65\x6E\x63\x65\x5F\x75\x69\x20\x7B\x62\x6F\x78\x2D\x73\x68\x61\x64\x6F\x77\x3A\x20\x30\x20\x30\x20\x33\x65\x6D\x20\x31\x70\x78\x20\x23\x30\x30\x30\x7D\x0A\x0A\x23\x62\x75\x64\x64\x79\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x68\x61\x6E\x64\x6C\x65\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x6F\x63\x75\x73\x65\x64\x20\x20\x7B\x62\x6F\x78\x2D\x73\x68\x61\x64\x6F\x77\x3A\x20\x30\x20\x30\x20\x33\x70\x78\x20\x23\x30\x30\x30\x2C\x69\x6E\x73\x65\x74\x20\x30\x20\x30\x20\x33\x70\x78\x20\x23\x30\x30\x30\x2C\x30\x20\x30\x20\x33\x65\x6D\x20\x35\x70\x78\x20\x23\x66\x66\x66\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x69\x64\x65\x4E\x61\x76\x43\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x6A\x65\x77\x65\x6C\x43\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x78\x74\x75\x61\x6C\x44\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x43\x61\x70\x73\x75\x6C\x65\x20\x2E\x66\x62\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x54\x77\x6F\x43\x6F\x6C\x75\x6D\x6E\x20\x3E\x20\x2E\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x55\x6E\x69\x74\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x52\x65\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x4F\x76\x65\x72\x6C\x61\x79\x50\x61\x67\x65\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x67\x65\x73\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x50\x61\x67\x65\x6C\x65\x74\x20\x2E\x63\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x65\x72\ x2E\x66\x62\x78\x5F\x62\x61\x72\x20\x23\x70\x72\x65\x73\x65\x6E\x63\x65\x5F\x75\x69\x20\x23\x70\x72\x65\x73\x65\x6E\x63\x65\x5F\x62\x61\x72\x20\x2E\x68\x69\x67\x68\x6C\x69\x67\x68\x74\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x4E\x75\x62\x46\x6C\x79\x6F\x75\x74\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x63\x61\x72\x64\x20\x2E\x73\x74\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x23\x66\x62\x44\x6F\x63\x6B\x43\x68\x61\x74\x42\x75\x64\x64\x79\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x4E\x75\x62\x20\x2E\x66\x62\x4E\x75\x62\x46\x6C\x79\x6F\x75\x74\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x62\x61\x6C\x6C\x6F\x6F\x6E\x2D\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x2D\x63\x78\x2D\x50\x52\x49\x56\x41\x54\x45\x2D\x75\x69\x44\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x5F\x5F\x62\x6F\x72\x64\x65\x72\x20\x20\x7B\x62\x6F\x78\x2D\x73\x68\x61\x64\x6F\x77\x3A\x20\x30\x20\x30\x20\x33\x65\x6D\x20\x35\x70\x78\x20\x23\x39\x63\x66\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x2E\x66\x62\x4E\x75\x62\x46\x6C\x79\x6F\x75\x74\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x4D\x65\x6E\x75\x58\x42\x6F\x72\x64\x65\x72\x20\x7B\x62\x6F\x78\x2D\x73\x68\x61\x64\x6F\x77\x3A\x20\x30\x20\x30\x20\x33\x65\x6D\x20\x35\x70\x78\x20\x23\x30\x30\x30\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x23\x62\x6C\x75\x65\x42\x61\x72\x20\x7B\x62\x6F\x78\x2D\x73\x68\x61\x64\x6F\x77\x3A\x20\x30\x20\x30\x20\x31\x65\x6D\x20\x33\x70\x78\x20\x23\x30\x30\x30\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x0A\x2E\x66\x69\x6C\x6C\x20\x7B\x62\x6F\x78\x2D\x73\x68\x61\x64\x6F\x77\x3A\x20\x69\x6E\x73\x65\x74\x20\x30\x20\x30\x20\x32\x65\x6D\x20\x23\x36\x39\x66\x2C\x30\x20\x30\x20\x31\x65\x6D\x20\x23\x30\x30\x30\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x0A\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x22\x5D\x7B\x2D\x6D\x6F\x7A\x2D\x61\x70\x70\x65\x61\x72\x61\x6E\x63\x65\x3A\x6E\x6F\x6E\x65\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x62\x6F\x72\x64\x65\x72\x3A\x20\x6E\x6F\x6E\x65\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x0A\x2E\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x5F\x74\x65\x78\ x5F\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x5F\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x6D\x65\x67\x61\x70\x68\x6F\x6E\x65\x5F\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x73\x6F\x75\x72\x63\x65\x5F\x6E\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x41\x74\x74\x61\x63\x68\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x4C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x66\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x3E\x20\x2E\x66\x6E\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x23\x70\x72\x65\x73\x65\x6E\x63\x65\x5F\x61\x70\x70\x6C\x69\x63\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x2C\x2E\x6D\x66\x73\x5F\x65\x6D\x61\x69\x6C\x5F\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x6C\x79\x6F\x75\x74\x20\x2E\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x4C\x69\x6E\x6B\x20\x2E\x55\x49\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x61\x6E\x6E\x6F\x75\x6E\x63\x65\x5F\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x61\x74\x74\x61\x63\x68\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x20\x61\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6D\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x61\x75\x74\x68\x6F\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x50\x6F\x72\x74\x72\x61\x69\x74\x5F\x54\x65\x78\x74\x20\x2E\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6D\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x49\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x61\x6C\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x4E\x61\x6D\x65\x73\x2C\x23\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x5F\x6E\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x5F\x54\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x64\x68\x5F\x6E\x65\x77\x5F\x6D\x65\x64\x69\x61\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x73\x68\x61\x72\x65\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x5F\x62\x72\x6F\x77\x73\x65\x72\x20\x64\x69\x76\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x41\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x4D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x54\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4E\x65\x73\x74\x65\x64\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x6C\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x73\x74\x61\x74\x5F\x65\x6C\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x23\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x63\x74\x5F\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x65\x72\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x20\ x62\x5F\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x6C\x69\x6B\x65\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x61\x2E\x55\x49\x49\x6D\x61\x67\x65\x42\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x54\x79\x70\x65\x61\x68\x65\x61\x64\x56\x69\x65\x77\x20\x6C\x69\x20\x2E\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x61\x75\x74\x68\x6F\x72\x2C\x2E\x61\x75\x74\x68\x6F\x72\x73\x2C\x2E\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x4C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x73\x73\x69\x76\x65\x4E\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x6B\x65\x6E\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x43\x75\x72\x72\x65\x6E\x74\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x53\x65\x74\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x73\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x4C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x49\x63\x6F\x6E\x54\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x23\x75\x65\x74\x71\x67\x31\x5F\x38\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x52\x65\x6D\x69\x6E\x64\x65\x72\x73\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x6D\x6C\x65\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x4D\x65\x6E\x75\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x20\x2E\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x20\x2E\x6E\x61\x6D\x65\x20\x20\x7B\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x23\x39\x63\x66\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x23\x65\x6D\x61\x69\x6C\x2C\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x64\x69\x73\x63\x6C\x61\x69\x6D\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x20\x64\x64\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x55\x70\x63\x6F\x6D\x69\x6E\x67\x5F\x49\x6E\x66\x6F\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x54\x6F\x73\x5F\x52\x65\x76\x69\x65\x77\x44\x65\x73\x63\x72\x69\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x73\x65\x74\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x73\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x5F\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x64\x69\x76\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x28\x38\x35\x2C\x38\x35\x2C\x38\x35\x29\x22\x5D\x20\x7B\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x23\x39\x39\x39\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x2E\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x5F\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x5F\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x5F\x77\x72\x61\x70\x70\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x70\x79\x72\x69\x67\x68\x74\x2C\x23\x6E\x65\x77\x73\x66\x65\x65\x64\x5F\x73\x75\x62\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x2C\x23\x6E\x65\x77\x73\x66\x65\x65\x64\x5F\x73\x75\ x6E\x2C\x23\x6E\x6F\x5F\x6E\x6F\x74\x65\x73\x2C\x23\x63\x68\x65\x61\x74\x5F\x73\x68\x65\x65\x74\x2C\x2E\x66\x6F\x72\x6D\x5F\x6C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x73\x68\x61\x72\x65\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x5F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x2C\x2E\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x5F\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x78\x5F\x73\x75\x62\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x72\x65\x76\x69\x65\x77\x5F\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x5F\x73\x75\x62\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x2C\x2E\x73\x75\x6D\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x20\x73\x74\x72\x6F\x6E\x67\x2C\x2E\x75\x70\x73\x65\x6C\x6C\x20\x64\x64\x2C\x2E\x61\x76\x61\x69\x6C\x61\x62\x69\x6C\x69\x74\x79\x5F\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x23\x70\x75\x62\x6C\x69\x63\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x5F\x61\x6C\x62\x75\x6D\x2C\x2E\x65\x78\x70\x6C\x61\x6E\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x61\x69\x6D\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x73\x75\x62\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x23\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x2C\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x28\x35\x31\x2C\x35\x31\x2C\x35\x31\x29\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x66\x70\x68\x6F\x6E\x65\x5F\x6C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x70\x68\x6F\x6E\x65\x5F\x74\x79\x70\x65\x5F\x6C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x73\x75\x62\x6C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x67\x69\x66\x74\x5F\x63\x61\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x64\x64\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x65\x76\x65\x6E\x74\x73\x5F\x62\x61\x72\x2C\x2E\x73\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x69\x6E\x67\x2C\x2E\x65\x76\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x5F\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x65\x65\x64\x42\x61\x63\x6B\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x6E\x64\x2C\x2E\x66\x70\x5F\x73\x68\x6F\x77\x5F\x6C\x65\x73\x73\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x63\x72\x65\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x73\x20\x74\x64\x2C\x2E\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x66\x69\x72\x6D\x2C\x2E\x73\x65\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x63\x65\x2C\x2E\x61\x64\x6D\x69\x6E\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x61\x72\x64\x6B\x69\x74\x5F\x6E\x6F\x5F\x74\x6F\x70\x69\x63\x73\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x61\x72\x64\x6B\x69\x74\x5F\x73\x75\x62\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\ x6D\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x70\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x2C\x2E\x67\x75\x65\x73\x74\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x2C\x2E\x6E\x6F\x5F\x70\x61\x67\x65\x73\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x70\x69\x63\x5F\x70\x61\x67\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x5F\x63\x6F\x6D\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x64\x69\x76\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x28\x31\x30\x31\x2C\x31\x30\x37\x2C\x31\x31\x31\x29\x22\x5D\x2C\x23\x71\x2C\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x28\x38\x35\x2C\x38\x35\x2C\x38\x35\x29\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x70\x6C\x2D\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x67\x67\x65\x64\x5F\x69\x6E\x2C\x2E\x70\x69\x63\x6B\x5F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x74\x64\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x28\x38\x35\x2C\x38\x35\x2C\x38\x35\x29\x22\x5D\x2C\x73\x74\x72\x6F\x6E\x67\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x28\x36\x38\x2C\x36\x38\x2C\x36\x38\x29\x22\x5D\x2C\x64\x69\x76\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x67\x72\x61\x79\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x5F\x6F\x66\x66\x69\x63\x65\x72\x73\x20\x64\x64\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x70\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x5F\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x61\x70\x70\x6C\x69\x63\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x64\x69\x76\x69\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x6D\x6F\x72\x65\x5F\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x2C\x2E\x6C\x6F\x67\x67\x65\x64\x5F\x6F\x75\x74\x5F\x72\x65\x67\x69\x73\x74\x65\x72\x5F\x73\x75\x62\x68\x65\x61\x64\x2C\x2E\x6C\x6F\x67\x67\x65\x64\x5F\x6F\x75\x74\x5F\x72\x65\x67\x69\x73\x74\x65\x72\x5F\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x65\x72\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x74\x65\x78\x74\x22\x5D\x2C\x74\x65\x78\x74\x61\x72\x65\x61\x2C\x2E\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x5F\x6E\x61\x6D\x65\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x22\x5D\x2C\ x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x22\x5D\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x5B\x76\x61\x6C\x75\x65\x3D\x22\x43\x6F\x6D\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x22\x5D\x29\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x70\x61\x73\x73\x77\x6F\x72\x64\x22\x5D\x2C\x23\x72\x65\x67\x5F\x70\x61\x67\x65\x73\x5F\x6D\x73\x67\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4D\x75\x74\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x54\x69\x70\x2C\x2E\x6C\x69\x6B\x65\x5F\x73\x65\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x63\x65\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x49\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x61\x6C\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x49\x6E\x66\x6F\x54\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x48\x6F\x74\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x57\x68\x79\x2C\x2E\x71\x75\x65\x73\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x6B\x65\x6E\x69\x7A\x65\x72\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x68\x69\x64\x64\x65\x6E\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x6B\x65\x6E\x69\x7A\x65\x72\x5F\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x20\x2A\x2C\x2E\x74\x65\x78\x74\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x65\x78\x74\x65\x72\x6E\x61\x6C\x29\x2C\x2E\x66\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x65\x64\x69\x74\x20\x62\x2C\x2E\x66\x65\x78\x74\x68\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x41\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x4D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x4D\x61\x69\x6E\x2C\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x28\x31\x30\x32\x2C\x31\x30\x32\x2C\x31\x30\x32\x29\x22\x5D\x2C\x64\x69\x76\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x28\x38\x35\x2C\x38\x35\x2C\x38\x35\x29\x22\x5D\x2C\x64\x69\x76\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x28\x31\x31\x39\x2C\x31\x31\x39\x2C\x31\x31\x39\x29\x22\x5D\x2C\x62\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x71\x75\x6F\x74\x65\x2C\x2E\x64\x65\x73\x63\x72\x69\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x73\x65\x63\x75\x72\x69\x74\x79\x5F\x62\x61\x64\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x75\x6C\x6C\x5F\x6E\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x65\x6D\x61\x69\x6C\x5F\x64\x69\x73\x70\x6C\x61\x79\x2C\x2E\x65\x6D\x61\x69\x6C\x5F\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x63\x68\x61\x74\x5F\x66\x6C\x5F\x6E\x75\x78\x5F\x6D\x65\x73\x73\x61\ x5F\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x65\x78\x63\x65\x72\x70\x74\x2C\x2E\x64\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x5F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x73\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x45\x4D\x55\x41\x53\x46\x72\x61\x6D\x65\x5F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x6E\x6F\x74\x65\x2C\x2E\x6E\x75\x78\x5F\x68\x69\x67\x68\x6C\x69\x67\x68\x74\x5F\x63\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x49\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x61\x6C\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x42\x6F\x74\x74\x6F\x6D\x41\x74\x74\x72\x69\x62\x75\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x67\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x2C\x2E\x47\x42\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x2C\x2E\x67\x69\x67\x61\x62\x6F\x78\x78\x5F\x74\x68\x72\x65\x61\x64\x5F\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x5F\x61\x75\x74\x68\x6F\x72\x73\x2C\x2E\x47\x42\x54\x68\x72\x65\x61\x64\x4D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x52\x6F\x77\x5F\x52\x65\x66\x65\x72\x72\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x23\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x65\x72\x57\x72\x61\x70\x70\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x67\x5F\x65\x78\x70\x6C\x61\x69\x6E\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4D\x65\x6E\x74\x6F\x72\x5F\x4D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x47\x65\x6E\x65\x72\x69\x63\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x42\x6F\x74\x74\x6F\x6D\x41\x74\x74\x72\x69\x62\x75\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x63\x68\x61\x74\x5F\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x2C\x2E\x76\x69\x64\x65\x6F\x5F\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x73\x74\x61\x6D\x70\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x23\x74\x61\x67\x67\x65\x72\x5F\x70\x72\x6F\x6D\x70\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x49\x6D\x61\x67\x65\x42\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x6E\x65\x77\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x20\x2E\x47\x42\x53\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x42\x6F\x78\x5F\x49\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x20\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x2C\x2E\x53\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x50\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x45\x6D\x61\x69\x6C\x53\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x4C\x65\x66\x74\x2C\x2E\x73\x75\x62\x5F\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x42\x69\x67\x4E\x75\x6D\x62\x65\x72\x5F\x4C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x49\x6E\x73\x69\x67\x68\x74\x73\x47\x65\x6F\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\ x73\x69\x67\x68\x74\x73\x54\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x20\x74\x64\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x6C\x6C\x5F\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x5F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x74\x72\x65\x61\x6D\x50\x61\x73\x73\x69\x76\x65\x2C\x2E\x73\x6E\x69\x70\x70\x65\x74\x2C\x2E\x71\x75\x65\x73\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x49\x6E\x66\x6F\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x6F\x6D\x6F\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x48\x6F\x77\x74\x6F\x2C\x2E\x66\x63\x67\x2C\x2E\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x43\x6F\x6C\x75\x6D\x6E\x20\x2E\x66\x77\x62\x2C\x2E\x72\x6F\x77\x47\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x20\x2E\x66\x77\x62\x2C\x2E\x72\x6F\x77\x47\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x44\x65\x73\x63\x72\x69\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x20\x2E\x66\x77\x62\x2C\x2E\x6C\x69\x6B\x65\x55\x6E\x69\x74\x2C\x2E\x61\x62\x6F\x76\x65\x55\x6E\x69\x74\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x70\x6C\x61\x63\x65\x68\x6F\x6C\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x46\x61\x71\x5F\x53\x6E\x69\x70\x70\x65\x74\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x4D\x65\x6E\x75\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x63\x68\x65\x63\x6B\x65\x64\x29\x20\x2E\x6E\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x62\x61\x6C\x6C\x6F\x6F\x6E\x2D\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x4C\x6F\x6E\x67\x42\x6C\x75\x72\x62\x2C\x2E\x6C\x65\x67\x65\x6E\x64\x4C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x6D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x42\x6F\x64\x79\x20\x7B\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x23\x62\x62\x62\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x2E\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x5F\x63\x6C\x65\x61\x72\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x68\x33\x2C\x68\x31\x2C\x2E\x75\x70\x64\x61\x74\x65\x73\x2C\x2E\x57\x65\x6C\x63\x6F\x6D\x65\x50\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x53\x69\x67\x6E\x55\x70\x48\x65\x61\x64\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x2C\x2E\x57\x65\x6C\x63\x6F\x6D\x65\x50\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x53\x69\x67\x6E\x55\x70\x53\x75\x62\x68\x65\x61\x64\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x2C\x2E\x6D\x6F\x63\x6B\x5F\x68\x34\x20\x2E\x6C\x65\x66\x74\x2C\x2E\x72\x65\x76\x69\x65\x77\x5F\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x5F\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x63\x61\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x6C\x6F\x67\x67\x65\x64\x5F\x6F\x75\x74\x5F\x72\x65\x67\x69\ x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x72\x65\x6D\x6F\x76\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x67\x69\x6E\x6F\x72\x6D\x6F\x75\x73\x50\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x4E\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x65\x78\x70\x65\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x63\x65\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x2E\x66\x77\x62\x2C\x23\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x74\x5F\x70\x6F\x70\x75\x6C\x61\x72\x5F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x20\x64\x69\x76\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x23\x38\x38\x30\x30\x30\x30\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x66\x73\x6D\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x73\x6E\x69\x70\x70\x65\x74\x29\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x4C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x29\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x66\x62\x43\x68\x61\x74\x4D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x29\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x74\x72\x65\x61\x6D\x48\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x54\x65\x78\x74\x52\x69\x67\x68\x74\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x6F\x6B\x6D\x61\x72\x6B\x73\x4E\x61\x76\x53\x65\x65\x41\x6C\x6C\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x20\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x50\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x50\x6C\x61\x63\x65\x73\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x43\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x4D\x61\x72\x6B\x65\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x54\x65\x78\x74\x43\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x44\x61\x72\x6B\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x67\x65\x4E\x75\x6D\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x70\x6C\x75\x67\x69\x6E\x52\x65\x63\x6F\x6D\x6D\x65\x6E\x64\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x42\x61\x72\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x20\x7B\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x23\x36\x39\x66\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x2E\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x73\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x63\x6F\x6D\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x62\x61\x63\x6B\x5F\x71\x75\x6F\x74\x65\x2C\x2E\x73\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x73\x6D\x61\x6C\x6C\x2C\x2E\x73\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x65\x78\x63\x65\x72\x70\x74\x2C\x2E\x77\x61\x6C\x6C\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x70\x75\x62\x6C\x69\x63\x2C\x70\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x23\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x73\x5F\x70\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x73\x75\x62\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x69\x6E\x5F\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x65\x6D\x70\x74\x79\x5F\x6D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x2C\ x65\x2C\x2E\x72\x73\x76\x70\x5F\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x6C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x42\x6C\x61\x63\x6B\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6D\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x61\x75\x74\x68\x6F\x72\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x66\x61\x6E\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x5F\x69\x6E\x61\x63\x74\x69\x76\x65\x2C\x2E\x68\x6F\x6C\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x54\x68\x75\x6D\x62\x50\x61\x67\x65\x72\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x72\x6F\x6C\x5F\x50\x61\x67\x65\x4E\x75\x6D\x62\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x74\x65\x78\x74\x5F\x63\x65\x6E\x74\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x6E\x6F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x5F\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x65\x6D\x61\x69\x6C\x5F\x70\x72\x6F\x6D\x69\x73\x65\x2C\x2E\x62\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x20\x75\x6C\x2C\x23\x61\x64\x76\x61\x6E\x63\x65\x64\x5F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x5F\x31\x20\x6C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x69\x6E\x75\x65\x2C\x2E\x65\x6D\x70\x74\x79\x5F\x61\x6C\x62\x75\x6D\x73\x2C\x64\x69\x76\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x62\x6C\x61\x63\x6B\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x47\x42\x54\x68\x72\x65\x61\x64\x4D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x52\x6F\x77\x5F\x42\x6F\x64\x79\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x53\x68\x61\x72\x65\x53\x74\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x53\x75\x62\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x23\x70\x75\x62\x6C\x69\x63\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x5F\x70\x68\x6F\x74\x6F\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x47\x65\x6E\x65\x72\x69\x63\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x4D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x41\x74\x74\x61\x63\x68\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x56\x61\x6C\x75\x65\x2C\x64\x69\x76\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x62\x6C\x61\x63\x6B\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x53\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x50\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x45\x6D\x61\x69\x6C\x53\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x54\x65\x78\x74\x53\x75\x62\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x6A\x65\x77\x65\x6C\x48\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x72\x65\x63\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x76\x69\x74\x79\x5F\x73\x65\x74\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x73\x5F\x6C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x70\x65\x6F\x70\x6C\x65\ x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x48\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x23\x61\x62\x6F\x75\x74\x5F\x74\x65\x78\x74\x5F\x6C\x65\x73\x73\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x53\x74\x72\x65\x61\x6D\x48\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x54\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x6E\x61\x76\x48\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x41\x74\x74\x61\x63\x68\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x50\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x50\x6C\x61\x63\x65\x73\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x54\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x67\x4E\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x75\x66\x62\x2D\x64\x61\x74\x61\x54\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x2D\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2D\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x75\x66\x62\x2D\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2D\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x43\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x41\x74\x74\x61\x63\x68\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x2E\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x20\x2E\x61\x74\x74\x61\x63\x68\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x4E\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x62\x61\x6C\x6C\x6F\x6F\x6E\x2D\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x63\x72\x6F\x70\x4D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x20\x7B\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x23\x66\x66\x66\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x2E\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x5F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x20\x7B\x6F\x70\x61\x63\x69\x74\x79\x3A\x20\x2E\x32\x35\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x2E\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x5F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x7B\x6F\x70\x61\x63\x69\x74\x79\x3A\x20\x31\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x2E\x76\x61\x6C\x69\x64\x2C\x2E\x77\x61\x6C\x6C\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x20\x73\x6D\x61\x6C\x6C\x2C\x23\x70\x68\x6F\x74\x6F\x64\x61\x74\x65\x2C\x2E\x76\x69\x64\x65\x6F\x5F\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x73\x74\x61\x6D\x70\x20\x73\x74\x72\x6F\x6E\x67\x2C\x2E\x64\x61\x74\x65\x5F\x64\x69\x76\x69\x64\x65\x72\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x66\x65\x65\x64\x5F\x6D\x73\x67\x20\x68\x35\x2C\x2E\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x73\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x61\x72\x64\x6B\x69\x74\x5F\x74\x6F\x70\x69\x63\x5F\x75\x70\x64\x61\x74\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x77\x61\x6C\x6C\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x65\x65\x64\x5F\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x73\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x2C\x23\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x5F\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x5F\x69\x6E\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x77\x72\x69\x74\x74\x65\x6E\x20\x73\x6D\x61\x6C\x6C\x2C\x2E\x64\x61\x74\x65\x2C\x64\x69\x76\x5B\x73\x74\x79\x6C\x65\x2A\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x28\x38\x35\x2C\x38\x32\x2C\x33\x37\x29\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x73\x74\x61\x6D\x70\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x6D\x70\x2C\x2E\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x73\x74\x61\x6D\x70\x2C\x2E\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x5F\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x5F\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x73\x74\x61\x6D\x70\x2C\x2E\x6D\x6F\x72\x65\x5F\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x20\x64\x69\x76\x2C\x2E\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x49\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x61\x6C\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x75\x70\x64\x74\x2C\x2E\x6E\x6F\x74\x65\x5F\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x73\x74\x61\x6D\x70\x2C\x2E\x63\x68\x61\x74\x5F\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x5F\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6D\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x49\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x61\x6C\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x20\x61\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x55\x70\x63\x6F\x6D\x69\x6E\x67\x5F\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x72\x69\x67\x68\x74\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x73\x2C\x2E\x47\x42\x54\x68\x72\x65\x61\x64\x4D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x52\x6F\x77\x5F\x44\x61\x74\x65\x2C\x2E\x47\x65\x6E\x65\x72\x69\x63\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x20\x61\x2C\x2E\x47\x65\x6E\x65\x72\x69\x63\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x50\x72\x69\x76\x61\x63\x79\x50\x61\x67\x65\x48\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x64\x61\x74\x65\x5F\x64\x69\x76\x69\x64\x65\x72\x20\x7B\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x23\x36\x39\x66\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x2E\x74\x65\x78\x74\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x2C\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x2C\x2E\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x64\x72\x6F\x70\x5F\x7A\x6F\x6E\x65\x2C\x2E\x6D\x73\x67\x5F\x64\x69\x76\x69\x64\x65\x5F\x62\x6F\x74\x74\x6F\x6D\x2C\x74\x65\x78\x74\x61\x72\x65\x61\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x74\x65\x78\x74\x22\x5D\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x22\x5D\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x73\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x22\x5D\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x22\x5D\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x70\x61\x73\x73\x77\x6F\x72\x64\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x73\x70\x61\x63\x65\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x6B\x65\x6E\x69\x7A\x65\x72\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x68\x69\x64\x64\x65\x6E\x22\x5D\x2C\x23\x66\x6C\x6D\x5F\x6E\x65\x77\x5F\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x54\x6F\x6F\x6C\x74\x69\x70\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x49\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x53\x68\x61\x64\x6F\x77\x2C\x2E\x73\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x72\x6F\x6F\x74\x20\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x6E\x61\x6D\x65\x3D\x22\x73\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x49\x6E\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x54\x6F\x6B\x65\x6E\x69\x7A\x65\x72\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x2E\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x2E\x6E\x6F\x73\x61\x76\x65\x20\x7B\x62\x61\x63\x6B\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x6E\x64\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x61\x28\x30\x2C\x30\x2C\x30\x2C\x2E\x35\x30\x29\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x2D\x6D\x6F\x7A\x2D\x61\x70\x70\x65\x61\x72\x61\x6E\x63\x65\x3A\x6E\x6F\x6E\x65\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x63\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3A\x20\x23\x62\x62\x62\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x62\x6F\x72\x64\x65\x72\x3A\x20\x6E\x6F\x6E\x65\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x70\x61\x64\x64\x69\x6E\x67\x3A\x20\x33\x70\x78\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x20\x7D\x0A\x0A\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x5B\x74\x79\ x49\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x6B\x65\x6E\x69\x7A\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x4C\x54\x6F\x6B\x65\x6E\x69\x7A\x65\x72\x57\x72\x61\x70\x2C\x23\x6D\x61\x69\x6C\x42\x6F\x78\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x73\x20\x6C\x69\x20\x61\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x54\x79\x70\x65\x61\x68\x65\x61\x64\x56\x69\x65\x77\x20\x2E\x73\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x20\x2E\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x41\x6E\x63\x68\x6F\x72\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x6E\x6F\x74\x65\x50\x65\x72\x6D\x61\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x4D\x61\x69\x6E\x63\x6F\x6C\x20\x2E\x74\x6F\x70\x5F\x62\x61\x72\x2C\x20\x2E\x6E\x6F\x74\x69\x66\x69\x63\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x61\x2C\x23\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x73\x20\x64\x69\x76\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x29\x2C\x2E\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x2C\x2E\x6E\x61\x76\x49\x64\x65\x6E\x74\x69\x74\x79\x20\x66\x6F\x72\x6D\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x6E\x65\x63\x74\x5F\x77\x69\x64\x67\x65\x74\x5F\x6E\x6F\x74\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x6E\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x5F\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x54\x79\x70\x65\x61\x68\x65\x61\x64\x56\x69\x65\x77\x20\x6C\x69\x2E\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x6E\x65\x63\x74\x5F\x77\x69\x64\x67\x65\x74\x5F\x6E\x75\x6D\x62\x65\x72\x5F\x63\x6C\x6F\x75\x64\x2C\x2E\x70\x6C\x61\x63\x65\x73\x4D\x61\x73\x68\x43\x61\x6E\x64\x69\x64\x61\x74\x65\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x68\x69\x67\x68\x6C\x69\x67\x68\x74\x2C\x23\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x20\x6C\x69\x20\x61\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x20\x7B\x62\x61\x63\x6B\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x6E\x64\x3A\x20\x72\x67\x62\x61\x28\x30\x2C\x30\x2C\x30\x2C\x2E\x35\x29\x20\x21\x69\x6D\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x61\x6E\x74\x3B\x7D\x0A\x0A\x2E\x72\x65\x73\x75\x6C\x74\x73\x20\x2E\x70\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x63\x61\x6C\x6C\x74\x6F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x72\x65\x73\x75\x6C\x74\x73\x20\x6C\x69\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x4E\x75\x62\x46\x6C\x79\x6F\x75\x74\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x78\x74\x75\x61\ x6F\x67\x2C\x2E\x64\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x2D\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x2E\x4C\x44\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x2C\x2E\x4C\x4A\x53\x44\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x2C\x2E\x64\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x2D\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x2C\x2E\x63\x68\x61\x74\x5F\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x2C\x23\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x43\x6F\x6C\x2C\x23\x6C\x65\x66\x74\x43\x6F\x6C\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x53\x74\x61\x6E\x64\x61\x72\x64\x46\x72\x61\x6D\x65\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x72\x65\x64\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x79\x65\x6C\x6C\x6F\x77\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x57\x61\x73\x68\x4C\x61\x79\x6F\x75\x74\x4F\x66\x66\x73\x65\x74\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x4F\x76\x65\x72\x6C\x61\x79\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x5F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x6E\x65\x63\x74\x5F\x77\x69\x64\x67\x65\x74\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x5F\x63\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x5F\x63\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x73\x68\x61\x64\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x6E\x61\x76\x49\x64\x65\x6E\x74\x69\x74\x79\x53\x75\x62\x2C\x2E\x6A\x65\x77\x65\x6C\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x20\x6C\x69\x20\x61\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x53\x69\x64\x65\x62\x61\x72\x47\x72\x69\x70\x70\x65\x72\x20\x64\x69\x76\x2C\x2E\x6A\x65\x77\x65\x6C\x43\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x42\x6F\x78\x52\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x76\x69\x64\x65\x6F\x55\x6E\x69\x74\x2C\x2E\x6C\x69\x66\x65\x45\x76\x65\x6E\x74\x41\x64\x64\x50\x68\x6F\x74\x6F\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x4C\x6F\x67\x49\x6E\x74\x72\x6F\x4D\x65\x67\x61\x70\x68\x6F\x6E\x65\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x47\x61\x6D\x65\x73\x4C\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x62\x6F\x61\x72\x64\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x67\x65\x73\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x50\x61\x67\x65\x6C\x65\x74\x20\x2E\x63\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x70\x61\x67\x65\x6C\x65\x74\x5F\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x5F\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x5F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x20\x2E\x63\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x6E\x65\x77\x49\x6E\x74\x65\ x65\x74\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x49\x6E\x66\x6F\x54\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x20\x2E\x6E\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x48\x43\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x73\x2C\x23\x64\x65\x76\x73\x69\x74\x65\x48\x6F\x6D\x65\x42\x6F\x64\x79\x20\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x64\x65\x76\x73\x69\x74\x65\x50\x61\x67\x65\x20\x2E\x6E\x61\x76\x20\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x23\x63\x6F\x6E\x66\x69\x72\x6D\x5F\x70\x68\x6F\x6E\x65\x5F\x66\x72\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x43\x61\x70\x73\x75\x6C\x65\x20\x2E\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x55\x6E\x69\x74\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x52\x65\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x61\x62\x6F\x76\x65\x55\x6E\x69\x74\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x61\x62\x6F\x75\x74\x4D\x65\x50\x61\x67\x65\x6C\x65\x74\x2C\x23\x70\x61\x67\x65\x6C\x65\x74\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x73\x2C\x23\x66\x62\x50\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x50\x6C\x61\x63\x65\x73\x42\x6F\x72\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x70\x61\x67\x65\x6C\x65\x74\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x6E\x6F\x74\x65\x73\x2C\x2E\x65\x78\x74\x65\x72\x6E\x61\x6C\x53\x68\x61\x72\x65\x55\x6E\x69\x74\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x4E\x61\x76\x69\x67\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x57\x72\x61\x70\x70\x65\x72\x20\x2E\x64\x65\x74\x61\x69\x6C\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x73\x50\x61\x6E\x65\x49\x6E\x66\x6F\x2C\x2E\x6E\x61\x76\x53\x75\x62\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x64\x6F\x6E\x61\x74\x65\x5F\x70\x61\x67\x65\x6C\x65\x74\x20\x3E\x20\x64\x69\x76\x2C\x2E\x62\x65\x74\x74\x65\x72\x5F\x66\x62\x5F\x6D\x69\x6E\x69\x5F\x6D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x42\x6F\x78\x57\x68\x69\x74\x65\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x4C\x6F\x61\x64\x69\x6E\x67\x49\x6E\x64\x69\x63\x61\x74\x6F\x72\x41\x73\x79\x6E\x63\x2C\x2E\x6D\x6C\x65\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x42\x6F\x78\x43\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x6E\x61\x76\x53\x75\x62\ x68\x6F\x6D\x65\x5F\x6D\x61\x69\x6E\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x66\x65\x65\x64\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x48\x6F\x6D\x65\x54\x61\x62\x73\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x2C\x23\x66\x65\x65\x64\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x61\x70\x70\x6C\x69\x63\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x20\x6C\x69\x2C\x2E\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x73\x65\x70\x61\x72\x61\x74\x6F\x72\x2C\x61\x5B\x68\x72\x65\x66\x3D\x22\x2F\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x73\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x66\x65\x65\x64\x5F\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x73\x68\x6F\x77\x5F\x61\x6C\x6C\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x2C\x23\x6E\x65\x77\x73\x66\x65\x65\x64\x5F\x73\x75\x62\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x2C\x2E\x6D\x6F\x72\x65\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x74\x6F\x67\x67\x6C\x65\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x6D\x6F\x72\x65\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x73\x2C\x2E\x62\x6C\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x2C\x2E\x73\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x65\x64\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x6C\x65\x66\x74\x5F\x63\x6F\x6C\x75\x6D\x6E\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x67\x65\x72\x5F\x6E\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x2E\x61\x64\x6D\x61\x72\x6B\x65\x74\x5F\x61\x64\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x73\x69\x64\x65\x2C\x2E\x73\x68\x61\x64\x65\x5F\x62\x2C\x2E\x77\x68\x6F\x5F\x63\x61\x6E\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x2C\x2E\x73\x75\x6D\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x5F\x73\x69\x6D\x70\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x65\x72\x5F\x73\x75\x62\x6D\x69\x74\x5F\x72\x6F\x75\x6E\x64\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x77\x65\x6C\x6C\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x5F\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x62\x61\x73\x69\x63\x5F\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x5F\x73\x75\x6D\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x5F\x61\x6E\x64\x5F\x76\x69\x65\x77\x65\x72\x5F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x20\x64\x74\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x20\x64\x74\x2C\x2E\x70\x68\x6F\x74\x6F\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x65\x78\x74\x72\x61\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x69\x6E\x5F\x63\ x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x65\x64\x69\x74\x70\x68\x6F\x74\x6F\x61\x6C\x62\x75\x6D\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x63\x68\x65\x63\x6B\x2C\x23\x6E\x65\x77\x61\x6C\x62\x75\x6D\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x61\x6C\x62\x75\x6D\x2C\x2E\x64\x68\x5F\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x62\x61\x72\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x64\x61\x73\x68\x62\x6F\x61\x72\x64\x5F\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x70\x68\x6F\x74\x6F\x73\x5F\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x69\x76\x61\x63\x79\x5F\x73\x75\x6D\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x73\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x69\x76\x61\x63\x79\x5F\x73\x75\x6D\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x62\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x5F\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x76\x69\x65\x77\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x69\x76\x61\x63\x79\x5F\x70\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x66\x69\x65\x6C\x64\x2C\x2E\x65\x64\x69\x74\x6F\x72\x5F\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x62\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x2C\x2E\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x65\x76\x65\x6E\x5F\x63\x6F\x6C\x75\x6D\x6E\x2C\x2E\x6D\x6F\x62\x69\x6C\x65\x5F\x61\x63\x63\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x5F\x69\x6E\x6C\x61\x79\x2C\x2E\x6C\x61\x6E\x67\x75\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x66\x69\x72\x6D\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x65\x73\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x66\x69\x72\x6D\x2C\x2E\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x66\x69\x72\x6D\x2C\x2E\x68\x61\x73\x6E\x74\x5F\x61\x70\x70\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x20\x2E\x55\x49\x44\x61\x73\x68\x62\x6F\x61\x72\x64\x48\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x5F\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x42\x61\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x44\x61\x73\x68\x62\x6F\x61\x72\x64\x48\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x6E\x6F\x74\x65\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x54\x77\x6F\x43\x6F\x6C\x75\x6D\x6E\x4C\x61\x79\x6F\x75\x74\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x64\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x5F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x2E\x64\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x73\x2C\x2E\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x73\x2C\x2E\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x73\x20\x74\x68\x2C\x2E\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\ x23\x70\x2D\x6C\x6F\x67\x6F\x2C\x23\x70\x2D\x6E\x61\x76\x69\x67\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x23\x70\x2D\x6E\x61\x76\x69\x67\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x20\x2E\x70\x42\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x23\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x68\x31\x2C\x23\x70\x2D\x77\x69\x6B\x69\x2C\x23\x70\x2D\x77\x69\x6B\x69\x20\x2E\x70\x42\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x23\x70\x2D\x73\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x2C\x23\x70\x2D\x73\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x20\x2E\x70\x42\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x23\x70\x2D\x74\x62\x2C\x23\x70\x2D\x74\x62\x20\x2E\x70\x42\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x23\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x74\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x2C\x23\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x74\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x20\x64\x69\x76\x2C\x2E\x72\x65\x63\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x6E\x65\x77\x73\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x69\x6E\x5F\x6E\x65\x77\x73\x2C\x2E\x6E\x65\x77\x73\x5F\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x20\x2E\x64\x65\x76\x73\x69\x74\x65\x5F\x73\x75\x62\x74\x61\x62\x73\x20\x6C\x69\x20\x61\x2C\x2E\x6D\x69\x64\x64\x6C\x65\x2D\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x65\x65\x64\x5F\x6D\x73\x67\x20\x68\x34\x2C\x2E\x61\x64\x73\x5F\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x63\x74\x5F\x73\x61\x6C\x65\x73\x2C\x2E\x77\x72\x61\x70\x70\x65\x72\x20\x68\x33\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x65\x73\x65\x6E\x63\x65\x5F\x62\x61\x72\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x69\x63\x6F\x6E\x5F\x67\x61\x72\x64\x65\x6E\x5F\x65\x6C\x65\x6D\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x5F\x6D\x69\x6E\x69\x66\x65\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x66\x6F\x63\x75\x73\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x64\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x5F\x73\x75\x6D\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x77\x61\x6C\x6C\x6B\x69\x74\x5F\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x68\x34\x2C\x2E\x61\x64\x64\x72\x65\x73\x73\x2C\x23\x62\x61\x64\x67\x65\x73\x2C\x2E\x62\x61\x64\x67\x65\x5F\x68\x6F\x6C\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x61\x69\x6D\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x75\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x2C\x2E\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x65\x64\x69\x74\x6F\x72\x2C\x2E\x6D\x79\x5F\ x6D\x61\x72\x79\x2C\x2E\x63\x61\x75\x73\x65\x2C\x20\x2E\x61\x74\x74\x61\x63\x68\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x61\x74\x74\x61\x63\x68\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x61\x72\x65\x61\x2C\x2E\x62\x65\x6E\x65\x66\x69\x63\x69\x61\x72\x79\x5F\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x2C\x23\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x2C\x23\x66\x65\x65\x64\x77\x61\x6C\x6C\x5F\x77\x69\x74\x68\x5F\x63\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x72\x6E\x69\x2C\x2E\x66\x72\x6E\x69\x20\x61\x2C\x2E\x66\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x65\x64\x69\x74\x2C\x2E\x66\x6D\x70\x5F\x64\x65\x6C\x65\x74\x65\x2C\x23\x66\x65\x65\x64\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x73\x20\x6C\x69\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x73\x20\x6C\x69\x3A\x6E\x6F\x74\x28\x2E\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x29\x2C\x2E\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x6C\x69\x20\x61\x2C\x2E\x76\x69\x65\x77\x5F\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x72\x6F\x75\x6E\x64\x65\x64\x2D\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x66\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x77\x72\x61\x70\x70\x65\x72\x5F\x62\x61\x63\x6B\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x6E\x64\x2C\x2E\x66\x75\x6C\x6C\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x77\x68\x69\x74\x65\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x23\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x73\x20\x6C\x69\x20\x61\x2C\x23\x69\x6E\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x5F\x63\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x73\x6B\x69\x6E\x5F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x76\x69\x74\x65\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x73\x69\x64\x65\x20\x74\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x74\x63\x68\x65\x73\x5F\x6D\x61\x74\x63\x68\x65\x73\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x74\x63\x68\x65\x73\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x5F\x73\x75\x62\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x74\x72\x5B\x66\x62\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x78\x74\x3D\x22\x34\x31\x30\x39\x37\x62\x66\x65\x62\x35\x38\x64\x22\x5D\x2C\x2E\x64\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x5F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x20\x64\x69\x76\x20\x64\x69\ x65\x5F\x77\x61\x6C\x6C\x5F\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x2C\x2E\x72\x65\x6C\x61\x74\x65\x64\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x68\x6F\x6D\x65\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x5F\x77\x72\x61\x70\x70\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x74\x77\x6F\x5F\x63\x6F\x6C\x75\x6D\x6E\x2C\x2E\x63\x68\x61\x6C\x6C\x65\x6E\x67\x65\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x74\x73\x2C\x2E\x71\x75\x69\x7A\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x20\x23\x66\x62\x5F\x63\x68\x61\x6C\x6C\x65\x6E\x67\x65\x2C\x23\x66\x62\x5F\x63\x68\x61\x6C\x6C\x65\x6E\x67\x65\x5F\x70\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x63\x68\x61\x6C\x6C\x65\x6E\x67\x65\x5F\x6C\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x62\x6F\x61\x72\x64\x2C\x2E\x6C\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x62\x6F\x61\x72\x64\x5F\x74\x69\x6C\x65\x2C\x20\x2E\x73\x69\x64\x65\x62\x61\x72\x5F\x75\x70\x73\x65\x6C\x6C\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x63\x65\x72\x74\x73\x5F\x6D\x6F\x64\x75\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x23\x6C\x6F\x67\x69\x6E\x5F\x68\x6F\x6D\x65\x70\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x75\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x68\x61\x74\x63\x68\x5F\x62\x67\x2C\x2E\x70\x69\x63\x6B\x5F\x6D\x61\x69\x6E\x2C\x23\x68\x6F\x6D\x65\x70\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x77\x61\x6C\x6C\x5F\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x5F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x2E\x74\x72\x61\x63\x6B\x2C\x2E\x48\x6F\x6D\x65\x54\x61\x62\x73\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x20\x61\x2C\x2E\x6D\x69\x6E\x69\x66\x65\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x61\x6C\x65\x72\x74\x5F\x77\x72\x61\x70\x2C\x2E\x6C\x6F\x67\x67\x65\x64\x5F\x69\x6E\x5F\x76\x65\x72\x74\x69\x63\x61\x6C\x5F\x61\x6C\x65\x72\x74\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x5F\x63\x6F\x6C\x75\x6D\x6E\x2C\x23\x70\x75\x62\x6C\x69\x63\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x5F\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x73\x2C\x23\x70\x75\x62\x6C\x69\x63\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x5F\x70\x61\x67\x65\x73\x2C\x2E\x67\x61\x6D\x65\x72\x74\x61\x67\x5F\x61\x70\x70\x2C\x2E\x67\x61\x6D\x65\x72\x50\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x42\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x23\x70\x68\x6F\x74\x6F\x5F\x70\x69\x63\x6B\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x61\x6C\x62\x75\x6D\x5F\x70\x69\x63\x6B\x65\x72\x20\x2E\x70\x61\x67\x65\x30\x20\x2E\x72\x6F\x77\x2C\x2E\x64\x69\x61\x6C\x6F\x67\x5F\x6C\x6F\x61\x64\x69\x6E\x67\x2C\x2E\x74\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\ x65\x6C\x63\x6F\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x73\x75\x6D\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x5F\x63\x75\x73\x74\x6F\x6D\x2C\x2E\x73\x6F\x75\x72\x63\x65\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x2C\x2E\x6D\x69\x6E\x6F\x72\x5F\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x41\x74\x74\x61\x63\x68\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x54\x44\x54\x65\x78\x74\x41\x72\x65\x61\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x5F\x64\x69\x66\x66\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x74\x63\x68\x65\x73\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x63\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x44\x72\x6F\x70\x64\x6F\x77\x6E\x5F\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x44\x72\x6F\x70\x64\x6F\x77\x6E\x5F\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x66\x65\x65\x64\x5F\x61\x75\x74\x6F\x5F\x75\x70\x64\x61\x74\x65\x5F\x73\x65\x74\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x73\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x73\x69\x6C\x76\x65\x72\x5F\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x5F\x67\x72\x69\x64\x5F\x63\x6F\x6C\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x6B\x65\x6E\x20\x3E\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x6B\x65\x6E\x69\x7A\x65\x72\x5F\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x6B\x65\x6E\x69\x7A\x65\x72\x5F\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x20\x2A\x2C\x23\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x73\x5F\x6D\x75\x6C\x74\x69\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x2C\x2E\x66\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x5F\x69\x6E\x6E\x65\x72\x20\x61\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x74\x79\x70\x65\x73\x2C\x23\x73\x74\x61\x72\x74\x61\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x20\x70\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x68\x65\x63\x6B\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x2C\x2E\x46\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x41\x64\x64\x69\x6E\x67\x54\x6F\x6F\x6C\x5F\x49\x6E\x6E\x65\x72\x4D\x65\x6E\x75\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x67\x65\x72\x70\x72\x6F\x20\x6C\x69\x20\x61\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x5F\x66\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x73\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x5F\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x63\x6F\x75\x6E\x74\x5F\x68\x6F\x6C\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x68\x70\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x76\x69\x65\x77\x5F\x61\x6C\x6C\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x61\x70\x70\x5F\x73\x65\x74\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x73\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x23\x66\x6C\x6D\x5F\x61\x64\x64\x5F\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x23\x66\x6C\x6D\x5F\x63\x75\x72\x72\x65\x6E\x74\x5F\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x2C\x23\x66\x6C\x6D\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x20\x2E\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x2C\x23\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x73\x5F\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x73\x5F\x77\x72\x61\x70\x70\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x63\x74\x73\x5F\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x63\x74\x73\x5F\x77\x72\x61\x70\x70\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x72\x6F\x77\x31\x2C\x2E\x73\x68\x6F\x77\x5F\x61\x64\x76\x61\x6E\x63\x65\x64\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x72\x6F\x6C\x73\x2C\x2E\x46\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x41\x64\x64\x69\x6E\x67\x54\x6F\x6F\x6C\x5F\x49\x6E\x6E\x65\x72\x4D\x65\x6E\x75\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x49\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x61\x6C\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x5F\x43\x6F\x6C\x6C\x61\x70\x73\x65\x64\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x69\x65\x73\x2C\x2E\x65\x6D\x61\x69\x6C\x5F\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x68\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x5F\x62\x67\x2C\x2E\x72\x71\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x61\x72\x5F\x68\x69\x67\x68\x6C\x69\x67\x68\x74\x2C\x23\x62\x75\x64\x64\x79\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x6C\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x2C\x2E\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x5F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x20\x61\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x63\x68\x61\x74\x5F\x73\x65\x74\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x20\x6C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x74\x6F\x6F\x6C\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x63\x68\x61\x74\x5F\x61\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x57\x65\x6C\x6C\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x49\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x41\x72\x65\x61\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x76\x69\x74\x65\x5F\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x61\x70\x69\x6E\x6F\x74\x65\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x49\x6E\x74\x65\x72\x73\x74\x69\x74\x69\x61\x6C\x42\x6F\x78\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x69\x63\x61\x6C\x5F\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x70\x73\x5F\x62\x72\x61\x6E\x64\x2C\x2E\x64\x69\x76\x62\x6F\x78\x34\x2C\x2E\x6C\x69\x67\x68\x74\x65\x72\x79\x65\x6C\x6C\x6F\x77\x2C\x2E\x66\x61\x6E\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x5F\x69\x6E\x61\x63\x74\x69\x76\x65\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x42\x65\x65\x70\x65\x72\x43\x61\x70\x2C\x2E\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x65\x72\x5F\x66\x61\x6C\x6C\x62\x61\x63\x6B\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x65\x72\x5F\x72\x65\x66\x69\x6E\x65\x5F\x73\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x5F\x63\x6F\x6D\x70\x61\x6E\x79\x5F\x73\x63\x68\x6F\x6F\x6C\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x65\x72\x5F\x72\x65\x66\x69\x6E\x65\x5F\x73\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x5F\x65\x6D\x61\x69\x6C\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4E\x65\x73\x74\x65\x64\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4E\x65\x73\x74\x65\x64\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x53\x75\x62\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4E\x65\x73\x74\x65\x64\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x5F\x4C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4E\x65\x73\x74\x65\x64\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x5F\x4C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4E\x65\x73\x74\x65\x64\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x53\x75\x62\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x5F\x4C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x61\x70\x70\x5F\x64\x69\x72\x5F\x61\x70\x70\x5F\x73\x75\x6D\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x2C\x2E\x61\x70\x70\x5F\x64\x69\x72\x5F\x66\x65\x61\x74\x75\x72\x65\x64\x5F\x61\x70\x70\x5F\x73\x75\x6D\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x2C\x2E\x61\x70\x70\x5F\x64\x69\x72\x5F\x61\x70\x70\x5F\x77\x69\x64\x65\x5F\x73\x75\x6D\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x5F\x74\x6F\x70\x5F\x62\x61\x72\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x53\x74\x72\x65\x61\x6D\x5F\x42\x6F\x72\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x71\x75\x65\x73\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x75\ x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x42\x6F\x78\x5F\x47\x72\x61\x79\x44\x61\x72\x6B\x54\x6F\x70\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x42\x6F\x78\x5F\x47\x72\x61\x79\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x42\x6F\x78\x2C\x23\x46\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x73\x50\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x56\x69\x65\x77\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x5F\x65\x64\x69\x74\x6F\x72\x2C\x2E\x65\x6E\x74\x72\x79\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x5F\x64\x61\x73\x68\x62\x6F\x61\x72\x64\x2C\x2E\x73\x70\x61\x63\x65\x79\x5F\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x74\x68\x72\x65\x61\x64\x2C\x2E\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x57\x61\x73\x68\x46\x72\x61\x6D\x65\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x74\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x5B\x62\x69\x6E\x64\x70\x6F\x69\x6E\x74\x3D\x22\x74\x68\x72\x65\x61\x64\x5F\x72\x6F\x77\x22\x5D\x2C\x74\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x5B\x62\x69\x6E\x64\x70\x6F\x69\x6E\x74\x3D\x22\x74\x68\x72\x65\x61\x64\x5F\x72\x6F\x77\x22\x5D\x20\x74\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x2E\x47\x42\x54\x68\x72\x65\x61\x64\x4D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x52\x6F\x77\x2C\x2E\x6D\x65\x73\x73\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x41\x72\x65\x61\x2C\x20\x2E\x55\x49\x52\x6F\x75\x6E\x64\x65\x64\x54\x72\x61\x6E\x73\x70\x61\x72\x65\x6E\x74\x42\x6F\x78\x5F\x42\x6F\x72\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x65\x65\x64\x62\x61\x63\x6B\x56\x69\x65\x77\x2C\x2E\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x2C\x2E\x73\x74\x72\x65\x61\x6D\x50\x61\x67\x69\x6E\x61\x74\x6F\x72\x2C\x2E\x6E\x75\x6C\x6C\x53\x74\x61\x74\x65\x50\x61\x6E\x65\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x62\x6F\x78\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x72\x6F\x6C\x73\x2C\x2E\x66\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x72\x6F\x6C\x73\x2C\x2E\x69\x6E\x62\x6F\x78\x56\x69\x65\x77\x20\x74\x72\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x56\x69\x65\x77\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x56\x69\x65\x77\x20\x6C\x69\x20\x61\x2C\x2E\x73\x70\x6C\x69\x74\x56\x69\x65\x77\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x70\x68\x6F\x74\x6F\x47\x72\x69\x64\x2C\x2E\x61\x6C\x62\x75\x6D\x47\x72\x69\x64\x2C\x2E\x66\x72\x61\x6D\x65\x20\ x69\x54\x65\x78\x74\x48\x69\x67\x68\x6C\x69\x67\x68\x74\x2C\x2E\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x72\x64\x65\x72\x65\x64\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x53\x65\x74\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x73\x50\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x50\x72\x69\x76\x61\x63\x79\x53\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x2D\x70\x61\x67\x65\x6C\x65\x74\x2D\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x49\x6E\x66\x6F\x53\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x23\x70\x74\x73\x5F\x69\x6E\x76\x69\x74\x65\x5F\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x69\x6E\x5F\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x73\x74\x65\x72\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x72\x6F\x6C\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x73\x74\x65\x72\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x72\x6F\x6C\x20\x2E\x6D\x61\x69\x6E\x2C\x2E\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x75\x69\x54\x79\x70\x65\x61\x68\x65\x61\x64\x56\x69\x65\x77\x20\x2E\x73\x65\x61\x72\x63\x68\x20\x6C\x69\x2C\x2E\x6C\x61\x6E\x67\x75\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x66\x6F\x72\x6D\x2C\x23\x61\x64\x73\x5F\x70\x72\x69\x76\x61\x63\x79\x5F\x65\x78\x61\x6D\x70\x6C\x65\x73\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x50\x72\x69\x76\x61\x63\x79\x50\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x53\x74\x61\x6E\x64\x61\x72\x64\x46\x72\x61\x6D\x65\x5F\x53\x69\x64\x65\x62\x61\x72\x41\x64\x73\x2C\x23\x73\x69\x64\x65\x62\x61\x72\x5F\x61\x64\x73\x2C\x23\x67\x6C\x6F\x62\x61\x6C\x57\x72\x61\x70\x70\x65\x72\x20\x23\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x70\x6F\x72\x74\x6C\x65\x74\x2C\x2E\x70\x42\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x2E\x6E\x6F\x61\x72\x74\x69\x63\x6C\x65\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x23\x63\x61\x74\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x73\x6D\x2C\x2E\x64\x65\x76\x73\x69\x74\x65\x48\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x64\x65\x76\x73\x69\x74\x65\x46\x6F\x6F\x74\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x64\x65\x76\x73\x69\x74\x65\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x62\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x2C\x2E\x62\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x20\x23\x74\x6F\x70\x69\x63\x2C\x2E\x62\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x20\x2E\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x6C\x65\x66\x74\x2C\x2E\x62\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x20\x2E\x70\x6F\x73\x74\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x6C\x65\ x6C\x69\x6E\x67\x42\x6F\x78\x3A\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x6A\x65\x77\x65\x6C\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x20\x6C\x69\x20\x61\x3A\x61\x63\x74\x69\x76\x65\x2C\x23\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x74\x69\x70\x5F\x70\x61\x67\x65\x6C\x65\x74\x20\x3E\x20\x64\x69\x76\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x55\x70\x63\x6F\x6D\x69\x6E\x67\x5F\x49\x74\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x76\x69\x64\x65\x6F\x5F\x77\x69\x74\x68\x5F\x63\x6F\x6D\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x73\x2C\x2E\x76\x69\x64\x65\x6F\x5F\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x46\x65\x65\x64\x54\x69\x63\x6B\x65\x72\x53\x74\x6F\x72\x79\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x46\x65\x65\x64\x54\x69\x63\x6B\x65\x72\x2E\x66\x69\x78\x65\x64\x5F\x65\x6C\x65\x6D\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x78\x50\x68\x6F\x74\x6F\x20\x2E\x66\x62\x50\x68\x6F\x74\x6F\x49\x6D\x61\x67\x65\x53\x74\x61\x67\x65\x20\x2E\x73\x74\x61\x67\x65\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x44\x65\x76\x65\x6C\x6F\x70\x65\x72\x41\x70\x70\x42\x6F\x64\x79\x20\x3E\x20\x2E\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x6F\x70\x65\x6E\x67\x72\x61\x70\x68\x20\x2E\x70\x72\x65\x76\x69\x65\x77\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x4E\x6F\x49\x6D\x61\x67\x65\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x53\x63\x72\x75\x62\x62\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x54\x69\x6D\x65\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x41\x64\x73\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x50\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x50\x6C\x61\x63\x65\x73\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x46\x65\x65\x64\x62\x61\x63\x6B\x50\x6F\x73\x74\x20\x2E\x55\x49\x49\x6D\x61\x67\x65\x42\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x2C\x2E\x70\x65\x72\x6D\x69\x73\x73\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x56\x69\x65\x77\x45\x64\x75\x63\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x46\x61\x71\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x23\x77\x69\x7A\x61\x72\x64\x2C\x2E\x63\x61\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x41\x72\x65\x61\x2C\x23\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x73\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x2E\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x62\x66\x62\x5F\x74\x61\x62\x5F\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x6F\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4D\ x6E\x64\x65\x64\x2C\x2E\x74\x6C\x2C\x2E\x74\x72\x2C\x2E\x6D\x6F\x64\x75\x6C\x65\x5F\x72\x69\x67\x68\x74\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x5F\x62\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x2C\x2E\x6D\x6F\x64\x75\x6C\x65\x5F\x62\x6F\x74\x74\x6F\x6D\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x2C\x2E\x6C\x6F\x63\x6B\x5F\x62\x5F\x62\x6F\x74\x74\x6F\x6D\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x2C\x23\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x5F\x73\x65\x63\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x5F\x32\x35\x33\x30\x30\x39\x36\x38\x30\x38\x20\x2E\x69\x6E\x66\x6F\x20\x64\x74\x2C\x2E\x70\x69\x70\x65\x2C\x2E\x64\x68\x5F\x6E\x65\x77\x5F\x6D\x65\x64\x69\x61\x2C\x2E\x64\x68\x5F\x6E\x65\x77\x5F\x6D\x65\x64\x69\x61\x20\x2E\x62\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x72\x6E\x5F\x69\x6E\x70\x61\x64\x2C\x23\x66\x72\x6E\x5F\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x73\x2C\x23\x66\x72\x6E\x69\x5F\x30\x2C\x2E\x66\x72\x65\x63\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x68\x33\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4D\x65\x64\x69\x61\x48\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x5F\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x57\x61\x73\x68\x2C\x2E\x65\x64\x69\x74\x6F\x72\x5F\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x6C\x20\x2E\x72\x69\x67\x68\x74\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4D\x65\x64\x69\x61\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x20\x74\x62\x6F\x64\x79\x20\x2A\x2C\x23\x75\x73\x65\x72\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x5F\x62\x6F\x78\x2C\x2E\x64\x61\x74\x65\x5F\x64\x69\x76\x69\x64\x65\x72\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x63\x6F\x72\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x70\x72\x6F\x66\x69\x6C\x65\x20\x23\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x65\x6E\x74\x20\x2E\x55\x49\x4F\x6E\x65\x4F\x66\x66\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x66\x66\x33\x2C\x2E\x70\x68\x6F\x74\x6F\x20\x23\x6E\x6F\x6E\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x65\x72\x20\x23\x70\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x68\x65\x69\x67\x68\x74\x2C\x2E\x68\x6F\x6D\x65\x20\x23\x6E\x6F\x6E\x66\x6F\x6F\x74\x65\x72\x20\x23\x70\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x68\x65\x69\x67\x68\x74\x2C\x2E\x68\x6F\x6D\x65\x20\x2E\x55\x49\x46\x75\x6C\x6C\x50\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x6D\x61\x69\x6E\x2D\x6E\x61\x76\x2C\x2E\x67\x65\x6E\x65\x72\x69\x63\x5F\x64\x69\x61\x6C\ x74\x6F\x72\x20\x2E\x61\x72\x72\x6F\x77\x20\x2E\x73\x65\x6C\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x20\x2E\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x20\x61\x2C\x2E\x6F\x6E\x6C\x69\x6E\x65\x5F\x73\x74\x61\x74\x75\x73\x5F\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x6C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x64\x72\x6F\x70\x5F\x7A\x6F\x6E\x65\x5F\x69\x6E\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x67\x6F\x6F\x64\x5F\x75\x73\x65\x72\x6E\x61\x6D\x65\x2C\x2E\x57\x65\x6C\x63\x6F\x6D\x65\x50\x61\x67\x65\x5F\x43\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x53\x68\x61\x72\x65\x42\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x20\x2A\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x4C\x69\x73\x74\x5F\x4C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x49\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x53\x68\x61\x64\x6F\x77\x20\x2E\x55\x49\x43\x6F\x6D\x70\x6F\x73\x65\x72\x5F\x54\x65\x78\x74\x41\x72\x65\x61\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4D\x65\x64\x69\x61\x48\x65\x61\x64\x65\x72\x5F\x54\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x57\x72\x61\x70\x70\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x78\x74\x6F\x70\x63\x6F\x6F\x6C\x5F\x68\x67\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x78\x74\x6F\x70\x63\x6F\x6F\x6C\x5F\x74\x72\x67\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x78\x74\x6F\x70\x63\x6F\x6F\x6C\x5F\x68\x64\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x78\x74\x6F\x70\x63\x6F\x6F\x6C\x5F\x74\x72\x64\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x78\x74\x6F\x70\x63\x6F\x6F\x6C\x5F\x62\x64\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x78\x74\x6F\x70\x63\x6F\x6F\x6C\x5F\x62\x67\x2C\x2E\x62\x6F\x78\x74\x6F\x70\x63\x6F\x6F\x6C\x5F\x62\x2C\x23\x63\x6F\x6E\x66\x69\x72\x6D\x5F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x2C\x2E\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x5F\x74\x65\x78\x74\x2C\x23\x61\x64\x76\x61\x6E\x63\x65\x64\x5F\x66\x72\x69\x65\x6E\x64\x73\x5F\x31\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x5F\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x2C\x2E\x66\x62\x5F\x6D\x65\x6E\x75\x5F\x69\x74\x65\x6D\x5F\x6C\x69\x6E\x6B\x20\x73\x6D\x61\x6C\x6C\x2C\x2E\x77\x68\x69\x74\x65\x5F\x68\x6F\x76\x65\x72\x2C\x2E\x47\x42\x54\x61\x62\x73\x65\x74\x5F\x50\x69\x6C\x6C\x20\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x2C\x2E\x55\x49\x4E\x65\x73\x74\x65\x64\x46\x69\x6C\x74\x65\x72\x4C\
